```python
from __future__ import annotations
import os
import logging
import uvicorn
from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from api.routes import router
from visualizer.app import router as visualizer_router
import os, sys
_root = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '../..'))
if _root not in sys.path:
    sys.path.insert(0, _root)
import config
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(name)s: %(message)s",
)
logger = logging.getLogger("engine")
app = FastAPI(
    title="Latent Diffusion-HMM Trading Engine",
    description=(
        "Quantitative trading signal pipeline implementing the v5.0 architecture: "
        "Unified HMM-Deep Learning Ensemble with VAE, Gumbel Router, and Meta-Learner."
    ),
    version="5.0.0",
    docs_url="/engine/redoc",
    redoc_url="/engine/api-docs",
    openapi_url="/engine/openapi.json",
)
allow_origins = config.CORS_ALLOWED_ORIGINS
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=allow_origins,
    allow_credentials=True if allow_origins != ["*"] else False,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)
app.include_router(router)
app.include_router(visualizer_router)
@app.get("/")
async def root():
    return {
        "engine": "Latent Diffusion-HMM v5.0",
        "docs": "/engine/redoc",
        "health": "/engine/healthz",
        "endpoints": [
            "POST /engine/analyze",
            "GET  /engine/regime/{ticker}",
            "POST /engine/signals",
            "POST /engine/features",
            "POST /engine/validate",
            "GET  /engine/docs-summary",
        ],
    }
if __name__ == "__main__":
    port = config.PORT
    logger.info(f"Starting Latent Diffusion-HMM engine on port {port}")
    uvicorn.run(
        "main:app",
        host="0.0.0.0",
        port=port,
        reload=False,
        log_level="info",
    )
```

## File: api/routes.py
```python
from __future__ import annotations
import logging
import traceback
from datetime import date, timedelta, datetime
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, BackgroundTasks
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, model_validator
import uuid
import os
import sys
_root = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '../..'))
if _root not in sys.path:
    sys.path.insert(0, _root)
import config
os.makedirs(config.RESULTS_DIR, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(os.path.join(config.RESULTS_DIR, ".hmm_cache"), exist_ok=True)
from v5_engine.pipeline_backtest import PipelineConfig, get_pipeline
logger = logging.getLogger("api")
router = APIRouter(prefix="/engine")
import pandas as pd
import glob
task_results: dict = {}
def _load_bars(ticker: str, start: str, end: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
    root = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "../.."))
    csv_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(root, "data", f"{ticker.lower()}*_1h*.csv"))
    if not csv_files:
        raise ValueError(f"No CSV data found for {ticker}")
    df = pd.read_csv(csv_files[0])
    df.columns = [c.lower() for c in df.columns]
    for tc in ["timestamp", "datetime", "time", "date"]:
        if tc in df.columns:
            if pd.api.types.is_numeric_dtype(df[tc]):
                df.index = pd.to_datetime(df[tc], unit='ms')
            else:
                df.index = pd.to_datetime(df[tc])
            df = df.drop(columns=[tc])
            break
    df.index.name = 'date'
    mask = (df.index >= pd.Timestamp(start)) & (df.index <= pd.Timestamp(end))
    return df[mask]
class AnalyzeRequest(BaseModel):
    ticker: str = Field(..., description="Ticker symbol, e.g. 'AAPL', 'SPY'")
    start: str = Field(
        default_factory=lambda: (date.today() - timedelta(days=365 * 3)).isoformat(),
        description="Start date ISO 8601, e.g. '2021-01-01'",
    )
    end: str = Field(
        default_factory=lambda: date.today().isoformat(),
        description="End date ISO 8601, e.g. '2024-01-01'",
    )
    equity: float = Field(default=100_000.0, ge=1.0, description="Portfolio equity in base currency")
    use_dollar_bars: bool = Field(default=True, description="Use dollar-volume bars (vs time bars)")
    apply_frac_diff: bool = Field(default=True, description="Apply fractional differentiation (MMMS)")
    run_validation: bool = Field(default=False, description="Run full statistical validation suite (slow)")
    n_mc_permutations: int = Field(default=200, ge=10, le=10000, description="Monte Carlo permutations")
    train_fraction: float = Field(default=0.7, ge=0.5, le=0.95)
    @model_validator(mode='after')
    def check_min_history(self) -> 'AnalyzeRequest':
        s = datetime.fromisoformat(self.start)
        e = datetime.fromisoformat(self.end)
        if (e - s).days < 730:
            raise ValueError("Engine mathematically requires at least 2 years (approx 504 bars) of history to fit Kalman window.")
        return self
class RegimeRequest(BaseModel):
    ticker: str
    lookback_days: int = Field(default=365, ge=30, le=365 * 10)
    @model_validator(mode='after')
    def check_minimum_lookback(self):
        if self.lookback_days < 180:
            raise ValueError("Minimum 180 days required for meaningful HMM fitting.")
        return self
class SignalRequest(BaseModel):
    ticker: str
    start: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: (date.today() - timedelta(days=365 * 2)).isoformat())
    end: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: date.today().isoformat())
    equity: float = Field(default=100_000.0)
class FeatureRequest(BaseModel):
    ticker: str
    start: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: (date.today() - timedelta(days=365 * 2)).isoformat())
    end: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: date.today().isoformat())
    n_bars: int = Field(default=50, ge=1, le=500)
class ValidateRequest(BaseModel):
    ticker: str
    start: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: (date.today() - timedelta(days=365 * 5)).isoformat())
    end: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: date.today().isoformat())
    n_mc_permutations: int = Field(default=500, ge=50, le=10000)
@router.get("/healthz")
async def health():
    import glob
    root_dir = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", ".."))
    csv_exists = len(glob.glob(os.path.join(root_dir, "data", "*_1h*.csv"))) > 0
    if not csv_exists:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail="Golden CSV dataset missing from disk! No data found.")
    return {"status": "ok", "engine": "Latent Diffusion-HMM v3.0", "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(), "csv_accessible": csv_exists}
def _run_pipeline_task(pipeline_cfg: PipelineConfig, task_id: str):
    try:
        pipeline = get_pipeline()
        result = pipeline.run(pipeline_cfg)
        task_results[task_id] = result.to_api_dict()
        logger.info(f"Task {task_id} completed successfully.")
    except Exception as e:
        task_results[task_id] = {"error": str(e)}
        logger.error(f"Task {task_id} failed: {e}")
@router.post("/analyze", status_code=202)
async def analyze(req: AnalyzeRequest, background_tasks: BackgroundTasks):
    try:
        pipeline_cfg = PipelineConfig(
            bars_df=_load_bars(req.ticker.upper(), req.start, req.end),
            ticker=req.ticker.upper(),
            start=req.start,
            end=req.end,
            equity=req.equity,
            use_dollar_bars=req.use_dollar_bars,
            apply_frac_diff=req.apply_frac_diff,
            run_validation=req.run_validation,
            n_mc_permutations=req.n_mc_permutations,
            train_fraction=req.train_fraction,
        )
        task_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
        background_tasks.add_task(_run_pipeline_task, pipeline_cfg, task_id)
        return {"status": "ACCEPTED", "task_id": task_id, "message": "Pipeline Walk-Forward started in background"}
    except ValueError as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(e))
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Pipeline error: {traceback.format_exc()}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Pipeline error: {str(e)}")
@router.get("/regime/{ticker}")
async def get_regime(ticker: str, lookback_days: int = 365):
    end = date.today().isoformat()
    start = (date.today() - timedelta(days=lookback_days)).isoformat()
    try:
        pipeline_cfg = PipelineConfig(
            bars_df=_load_bars(ticker.upper(), start, end),
            ticker=ticker.upper(),
            start=start,
            end=end,
            run_validation=False,
        )
        pipeline = get_pipeline()
        result = pipeline.run(pipeline_cfg)
        api = result.to_api_dict()
        return {
            "ticker": ticker.upper(),
            "current_regime": api["current_regime"],
            "regime_summary": api["regime_summary"],
            "surveillance": api["surveillance"],
            "n_bars": api["n_bars"],
            "recent_regimes": [
                {
                    "date": row["date"],
                    "regime": row["regime"],
                    "p_trend": row["p_trend"],
                    "p_mean_rev": row["p_mean_rev"],
                    "p_stress": row["p_stress"],
                }
                for row in api["feature_timeseries"][-20:]
            ],
        }
    except ValueError as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(e))
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(traceback.format_exc())
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
@router.post("/signals")
async def get_signals(req: SignalRequest):
    try:
        pipeline_cfg = PipelineConfig(
            bars_df=_load_bars(req.ticker.upper(), req.start, req.end),
            ticker=req.ticker.upper(),
            start=req.start,
            end=req.end,
            equity=req.equity,
            run_validation=False,
        )
        pipeline = get_pipeline()
        result = pipeline.run(pipeline_cfg)
        api = result.to_api_dict()
        return {
            "ticker": req.ticker.upper(),
            "period": {"start": req.start, "end": req.end},
            "n_signals": api["n_signals"],
            "signals": api["signals"],
            "current_regime": api["current_regime"],
        }
    except ValueError as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(e))
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(traceback.format_exc())
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
@router.post("/features")
async def get_features(req: FeatureRequest):
    try:
        pipeline_cfg = PipelineConfig(
            bars_df=_load_bars(req.ticker.upper(), req.start, req.end),
            ticker=req.ticker.upper(),
            start=req.start,
            end=req.end,
            run_validation=False,
        )
        pipeline = get_pipeline()
        result = pipeline.run(pipeline_cfg)
        api = result.to_api_dict()
        tail = api["feature_timeseries"][-req.n_bars:]
        return {
            "ticker": req.ticker.upper(),
            "n_bars": len(tail),
            "features": tail,
            "feature_descriptions": {
                "vt": "Volatility Proximity [-1, +1]. |vt| > 0.85 = breakout zone",
                "mvt": "Momentum Velocity (σ-gated log-momentum). |mvt| > 1.0 = signal",
                "qt": "Volume Delta Ratio. qt > 2.0 = institutional demand; < 0.5 = distribution",
                "sigma_t": "Volatility Regime Ratio (RV / GARCH). > 1.5 = jump precursor; < 0.6 = coiling",
                "rho_t": "Autocorrelation Signal. > 0.15 = trending; < -0.15 = mean-reverting",
                "ht": "DFA Hurst Exponent. > 0.55 = trend persistence; < 0.45 = mean reversion",
            },
        }
    except ValueError as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=str(e))
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(traceback.format_exc())
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))
@router.post("/validate")
async def validate(req: ValidateRequest):
    try:
        pipeline_cfg = PipelineConfig(

@router.get("/status/{task_id}")
async def get_status(task_id: str):
    result = task_results.get(task_id)
    if result is None:
        return {"status": "PENDING", "task_id": task_id}
    return {"status": "COMPLETE", "task_id": task_id, "result": result}
```

## File: data_pipeline/data_manager.py
```python
import os, sys
_root = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '../../'))
if _root not in sys.path: sys.path.insert(0, _root)
import config
import os
import asyncio
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
import tick_vault
PIPET_SCALES = config.PIPET_SCALES
class DataManager:
    def __init__(self, data_dir: str = "data"):
        self.data_dir = data_dir
        os.makedirs(self.data_dir, exist_ok=True)
        tick_vault.reload_config(base_directory=os.path.join(self.data_dir, "tick_vault_cache"))
    async def fetch_and_resample(self, symbol: str, start: datetime, end: datetime, timeframe: str = '1h'):
        print(f"\\n📡 Fetching Pristine Tick Data for {symbol}...")
        print(f"  -> Downloading missing .bi5 chunks...")
        try:
            await tick_vault.download_range(
                symbol=symbol,
                start=start,
                end=end,
            )
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"  [CRITICAL ERROR] Download failed for {symbol}: {e}")
            raise RuntimeError(f"Missing tick data causes mathematical failure. Aborting data generation for {symbol}.") from e
        print(f"  -> Reading ticks into RAM...")
        try:
            current_scale = PIPET_SCALES.get(symbol, 100000)
            df = tick_vault.read_tick_data(
                symbol=symbol,
                start=start,
                end=end,
                strict=False,
                show_progress=False,
                pipet_scale=current_scale
            )
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"❌ Failed to read data for {symbol}: {e}")
            return None
        if df.empty:
            print(f"❌ No data returned for {symbol}")
            return None
        print(f"  -> Resampling {len(df)} ticks into {timeframe} candles...")
        df['volume'] = df['ask_volume'] + df['bid_volume']
        df['signed_volume'] = df['bid_volume'] - df['ask_volume']
        df.set_index('time', inplace=True)
        ohlcv = df.resample(timeframe).agg({
            'bid': ['first', 'max', 'min', 'last'],
            'ask': ['first', 'max', 'min', 'last'],
            'volume': 'sum',
            'signed_volume': 'sum'
        }).dropna()
        ohlcv.columns = ['open_bid', 'high_bid', 'low_bid', 'close_bid',
                         'open_ask', 'high_ask', 'low_ask', 'close_ask',
                         'volume', 'signed_volume']
        ohlcv['open']  = (ohlcv['open_bid']  + ohlcv['open_ask'])  / 2
        ohlcv['high']  = (ohlcv['high_bid']  + ohlcv['high_ask'])  / 2
        ohlcv['low']   = (ohlcv['low_bid']   + ohlcv['low_ask'])   / 2
        ohlcv['close'] = (ohlcv['close_bid'] + ohlcv['close_ask']) / 2
        ohlcv['tib'] = ohlcv['signed_volume'] / (ohlcv['volume'].clip(lower=1e-10))
        ohlcv = ohlcv[['open', 'high', 'low', 'close', 'volume', 'tib']]
        ohlcv = ohlcv.reset_index()
        ohlcv = ohlcv.rename(columns={'time': 'timestamp'})
        ohlcv['timestamp'] = ohlcv['timestamp'].astype('datetime64[ms]').astype('int64')
        out_name = symbol.lower()
        out_path = os.path.join(self.data_dir, f"{out_name}_{timeframe}.csv")
        ohlcv.to_csv(out_path, index=False)
        print(f"✅ Saved pristine data to {out_path} ({len(ohlcv)} candles)")
        return ohlcv
async def main():
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Tick-Vault Dukascopy Downloader")
    parser.add_argument("--start", type=str, default="2020-01-01", help="Start date YYYY-MM-DD")
    parser.add_argument("--end", type=str, default="2024-12-31", help="End date YYYY-MM-DD")
    parser.add_argument("--symbols", type=str, default="EURUSD,XAUUSD,GBPUSD,AUDCAD,CHFJPY,EURNZD", help="Comma separated symbols")
    parser.add_argument("--timeframe", type=str, default="1h", help="Resample timeframe")
    args = parser.parse_args()
    manager = DataManager()
    start_date = datetime.strptime(args.start, "%Y-%m-%d")
    end_date = datetime.strptime(args.end, "%Y-%m-%d")
    print("=" * 60)
    print(" TICK-VAULT DATA ACQUISITION & RESAMPLING")
    print(f" Range: {args.start} to {args.end}")
    print("=" * 60)
    symbols = args.symbols.split(",")
    for sym in symbols:
        await manager.fetch_and_resample(sym, start_date, end_date, timeframe=args.timeframe)
    print("\\n✅ All assets downloaded and resampled successfully.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())
```

## File: diagnostics/audit_real_data.py
```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import traceback
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "v3_engine")))
from engine.features import compute_feature_tensor
from engine.preprocess import Preprocessor
from engine.hmm import TVTPHMM
from engine.surveillance import WassersteinMonitor
from engine.execution import SignalEngine
from engine.validation import _sharpe_ratio, monte_carlo_permutation_test
try:
    from engine.kalman import denoise_features
    HAS_KALMAN = True
except ImportError:
    HAS_KALMAN = False
def run_full_pipeline_audit(file_path="data/btcusd_1h.csv"):
    print("==================================================")
    print("🛡️ LATENT DIFFUSION-HMM: FULL 1-TO-6 PIPELINE AUDIT")
    print("==================================================\n")
    print("▶️ LAYER 1: Loading Real Market Data")
    try:
        df_raw = pd.read_csv(file_path)
        df_raw.columns = [c.lower() for c in df_raw.columns]
        if 'timestamp' in df_raw.columns:
            df_raw.index = pd.to_datetime(df_raw['timestamp'], unit='ms')
            df_raw.index.name = 'date'
            df_raw = df_raw.drop(columns=['timestamp'])
        elif 'date' in df_raw.columns:
            df_raw.index = pd.to_datetime(df_raw['date'])
            df_raw.index.name = 'date'
            df_raw = df_raw.drop(columns=['date'])
        df = df_raw.head(2000).copy()
        print(f"  ✅ LAYER 1 PASSED: Successfully loaded {len(df)} real bars.\n")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  ❌ LAYER 1 CRASHED: Ensure {file_path} exists.\n{e}\n")
        return
    print("▶️ LAYER 2: 6D Tensor & Welford Whitening")
    try:
        raw_features = compute_feature_tensor(df)
        pp = Preprocessor()
        clean_X = pp.fit_transform(raw_features)
        clean_mask = ~np.any(np.isnan(clean_X), axis=1)
        clean_X_valid = clean_X[clean_mask]
        mean_val = float(np.mean(clean_X_valid))
        std_val = float(np.std(clean_X_valid))
        if abs(mean_val) < 0.1 and abs(std_val - 1.0) < 0.1:
            print(f"  ✅ LAYER 2 PASSED: Tensor Normalized (Mean: {mean_val:.2f}, Std: {std_val:.2f})\n")
        else:
            print(f"  ❌ LAYER 2 FAILED: Normalization leaked. (Mean: {mean_val:.2f}, Std: {std_val:.2f})\n")
            return
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  ❌ LAYER 2 CRASHED:\n{traceback.format_exc()}\n")
        return
    print("▶️ LAYER 3: Kalman Denoising & CUSUM Detect")
    try:
        if HAS_KALMAN:
            denoised_X = denoise_features(clean_X_valid)
            print("  ✅ LAYER 3 PASSED: Features successfully passed through State-Space Filter.\n")
        else:
            denoised_X = clean_X_valid
            print("  ⚠️ LAYER 3 SKIPPED: Kalman module not imported, bypassing to Layer 4.\n")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  ❌ LAYER 3 CRASHED:\n{traceback.format_exc()}\n")
        return
    print("▶️ LAYER 4: TVTP-HMM Expectation-Maximization")
    try:
        covariates = denoised_X[:, -2:]
        hmm = TVTPHMM(n_states=3, n_gmm=2, n_iter=10)
        hmm.fit(denoised_X, covariates)
        proba = hmm.predict_proba(denoised_X, covariates)
        avg_proba = np.mean(proba, axis=0)
        if np.allclose(avg_proba, [0.333, 0.333, 0.333], atol=0.05):
            print("  ❌ LAYER 4 FAILED: HMM Math Collapsed to 0.333.\n")
            return
        else:
            print(f"  ✅ LAYER 4 PASSED: Clusters Found (Avg Prob: {avg_proba[0]:.2f}, {avg_proba[1]:.2f}, {avg_proba[2]:.2f})\n")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  ❌ LAYER 4 CRASHED:\n{traceback.format_exc()}\n")
        return
    print("▶️ LAYER 5: Execution Routing & Surveillance")
    try:
        monitor = WassersteinMonitor(window=50, w1_threshold_multiplier=0.3)
        monitor.fit(denoised_X[:1000])
        res = monitor.check(denoised_X[1000:1050])
        engine = SignalEngine()
        print(f"  ✅ LAYER 5 PASSED: Triple Gate Armed. Surveillance active (W1 Dist: {res['w1_distance']:.2f})\n")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  ❌ LAYER 5 CRASHED:\n{traceback.format_exc()}\n")
        return
    print("▶️ LAYER 6: Monte Carlo Permutation Test")
    try:
        real_returns = df['close'].pct_change().dropna().to_numpy()
        def dummy_simulate(returns): return _sharpe_ratio(returns)
        mc_res = monte_carlo_permutation_test(real_returns, dummy_simulate, n_permutations=100)
        print(f"  ✅ LAYER 6 PASSED: Permutation engine verified (Real Sharpe: {mc_res.actual_oos_sharpe:.2f})\n")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  ❌ LAYER 6 CRASHED:\n{traceback.format_exc()}\n")
        return
    print("==================================================")
    print("🏁 ALL 6 LAYERS MATHEMATICALLY VERIFIED")
    print("==================================================")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    parser.add_argument("--file", type=str, default="data/btcusd_1h.csv", help="Path to data CSV")
    args = parser.parse_args()
    run_full_pipeline_audit(args.file)
```

## File: live_trading/get_token.py
```python
import os
import sys
import requests
import os, sys
_root = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '../..'))
if _root not in sys.path:
    sys.path.insert(0, _root)
import config
def verify_environment_security():
    required_vars = ["CTRADER_CLIENT_ID", "CTRADER_CLIENT_SECRET", "CTRADER_AUTH_CODE", "ENVIRONMENT_MODE"]
    missing_vars = [var for var in required_vars if not os.getenv(var)]
    if missing_vars:
        print(f"[FATAL CRITICAL SECURITY FAILURE]: Missing Environment Parameters: {missing_vars}")
        sys.exit(1)
    forbidden_placeholders = ["PASTE_YOUR_AUTH_CODE_HERE", "dummy", "12345", "PLACEHOLDER"]
    for var in required_vars:
        value = os.getenv(var, "")
        if any(placeholder in value for placeholder in forbidden_placeholders):
            print(f"[FATAL SYSTEM INTEGRITY FAILURE]: Value for {var} contains dummy/placeholder strings.")
            sys.exit(1)
verify_environment_security()
CLIENT_ID = config.CTRADER_CLIENT_ID
CLIENT_SECRET = config.CTRADER_CLIENT_SECRET
REDIRECT_URI = "http://localhost:8080"
AUTH_CODE = config.CTRADER_AUTH_CODE
def get_access_token():
    print("🔄 Swapping Auth Code for Access Token...")
    token_url = "https://connect.spotware.com/oauth/v2/token"
    params = {
        "grant_type": "authorization_code",
        "code": AUTH_CODE,
        "redirect_uri": REDIRECT_URI,
        "client_id": CLIENT_ID,
        "client_secret": CLIENT_SECRET
    }
    response = requests.post(token_url, data=params)
    if response.status_code == 200:
        token_data = response.json()
        print("\n✅ SUCCESS! Here is your permanent Access Token:")
        print("="*60)
        print(token_data.get("accessToken"))
        print("="*60)
        print("\nPaste this token into the live_bridge_ctrader.py script!")
    else:
        print("\n❌ Failed to get token.")
        print(f"Status Code: {response.status_code}")
        print(f"Error: {response.text}")
        print("\nNote: Auth codes expire in 60 seconds! You might need to generate a new one from your browser.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    get_access_token()
```

## File: live_trading/live_bridge_ctrader.py
```python
import os
import sys
import asyncio
import json
import traceback
from datetime import datetime
import pandas as pd
from ctrader_open_api import Client, Protobuf, TcpProtocol, endpoints
from ctrader_open_api.messages.OpenApiCommonMessages_pb2 import *
from ctrader_open_api.messages.OpenApiMessages_pb2 import *
from ctrader_open_api.messages.OpenApiModelMessages_pb2 import *
_root = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '..'))
if _root not in sys.path:
    sys.path.insert(0, _root)
import config
from v3_engine.engine.pipeline import Pipeline, PipelineConfig
class CTraderLiveBridge:
    def __init__(self, client_id, client_secret, account_id, token, mode="demo"):
        self.client_id = client_id
        self.client_secret = client_secret
        self.account_id = account_id
        self.token = token
        self.host = endpoints.EndPoints.PROTOBUF_DEMO_HOST if mode == "demo" else endpoints.EndPoints.PROTOBUF_LIVE_HOST
        self.port = endpoints.EndPoints.PROTOBUF_PORT
        self.client = Client(self.host, self.port, TcpProtocol)
        self.pipeline = Pipeline()
        self.target_symbols = ["CHFJPY", "AUDCAD", "EURNZD"]
        self.symbol_ids = {}
        self.reverse_symbol_ids = {}
        self.ohlcv_cache = {}
        self.open_positions = {}
    def start(self):
        print(f"🚀 Connecting to cTrader Open API at {self.host}:{self.port}...")
        self.client.setConnectedCallback(self.on_connected)
        self.client.setDisconnectedCallback(self.on_disconnected)
        self.client.setMessageReceivedCallback(self.on_message_received)
        self.client.startService()
    def on_connected(self, client):
        print("✅ Connected to cTrader.")
        req = ProtoOAApplicationAuthReq()
        req.clientId = self.client_id
        req.clientSecret = self.client_secret
        self.client.send(req)
    def on_disconnected(self, client, reason):
        print(f"❌ Disconnected from cTrader: {reason}")
    def on_message_received(self, client, message):
        msg_type = message.payloadType
        if msg_type == 51:
            return
        if msg_type not in (2131, 2132, 2128):
            print(f"📩 DEBUG: Received Message Type: {msg_type}")
        if msg_type == ProtoOAApplicationAuthRes().payloadType:
            print("✅ Application Authorized. Fetching Accounts linked to this Token...")
            req = ProtoOAGetAccountListByAccessTokenReq()
            req.accessToken = self.token
            self.client.send(req)
        elif msg_type == ProtoOAGetAccountListByAccessTokenRes().payloadType:
            res = Protobuf.extract(message)
            print("✅ Token valid! Accounts linked to this token:")
            for acc in res.ctidTraderAccount:
                print(f"  -> Account ID: {acc.ctidTraderAccountId} | Live: {acc.isLive}")
            print(f"\nAuthenticating target account: {self.account_id}...")
            req = ProtoOAAccountAuthReq()
            req.ctidTraderAccountId = self.account_id
            req.accessToken = self.token
            self.client.send(req)
        elif msg_type == ProtoOAErrorRes().payloadType:
            res = Protobuf.extract(message)
            print(f"❌ cTrader API ERROR: {res.errorCode} - {res.description}")
        elif msg_type == ProtoOAExecutionEvent().payloadType:
            res = Protobuf.extract(message)
            pos = res.position
            if pos.positionStatus in [ProtoOAPositionStatus.POSITION_STATUS_CREATED, ProtoOAPositionStatus.POSITION_STATUS_OPEN]:
                self.open_positions[pos.tradeData.symbolId] = {
                    "positionId": pos.positionId,
                    "tradeSide": pos.tradeData.tradeSide,
                    "volume": pos.tradeData.volume
                }
            elif pos.positionStatus == ProtoOAPositionStatus.POSITION_STATUS_CLOSED:
                if pos.tradeData.symbolId in self.open_positions:
                    del self.open_positions[pos.tradeData.symbolId]
            print("\n" + "━"*55)
            print(f" 🛎️   LIVE DASHBOARD: BROKER EXECUTION EVENT")
            print("━"*55)
            print(res)
            print("━"*55 + "\n")
        elif msg_type == ProtoOAAccountAuthRes().payloadType:
            print(f"✅ Account {self.account_id} Authorized.")
            req = ProtoOAGetOpenPositionListReq()
            req.ctidTraderAccountId = self.account_id
            self.client.send(req)
            self.subscribe_to_symbols()
        elif msg_type == ProtoOAGetOpenPositionListRes().payloadType:
            res = Protobuf.extract(message)
            print("📊 Fetched Open Positions from cTrader:")
            for pos in res.position:
                self.open_positions[pos.tradeData.symbolId] = {
                    "positionId": pos.positionId,
                    "tradeSide": pos.tradeData.tradeSide,
                    "volume": pos.tradeData.volume
                }
                print(f"  -> Symbol ID: {pos.tradeData.symbolId} | Side: {'BUY' if pos.tradeData.tradeSide == ProtoOATradeSide.BUY else 'SELL'} | Vol: {pos.tradeData.volume}")
        elif msg_type == ProtoOASymbolsListRes().payloadType:
            res = Protobuf.extract(message)
            for symbol in res.symbol:
                if symbol.symbolName in self.target_symbols:
                    self.symbol_ids[symbol.symbolName] = symbol.symbolId
                    self.reverse_symbol_ids[symbol.symbolId] = symbol.symbolName
            print(f"📌 Resolved Symbol IDs: {self.symbol_ids}")
            self.fetch_historical_data()
            self.subscribe_to_spots()
        elif msg_type == ProtoOAOrderErrorEvent().payloadType:
            res = Protobuf.extract(message)
            print(f"❌ ORDER ERROR: {res.errorCode} - {res.description}")
        elif msg_type == ProtoOAMarginChangedEvent().payloadType:
            res = Protobuf.extract(message)
            print(f"⚠️ MARGIN ALERT: New Free Margin: {res.margin.freeMargin}")
        elif msg_type == ProtoOASpotEvent().payloadType:
            pass
        elif msg_type == ProtoOAGetTrendbarsRes().payloadType:
            res = Protobuf.extract(message)
            symbol_name = self.reverse_symbol_ids.get(res.symbolId, "UNKNOWN")
            print(f"📊 Received {len(res.trendbar)} historical bars for {symbol_name}")
            bars = []
            for b in res.trendbar:
                bars.append({
                    "time": pd.to_datetime(b.utcTimestampInMinutes * 60, unit='s'),
                    "open": b.low + b.deltaOpen,
                    "high": b.low + b.deltaHigh,
                    "low": b.low,
                    "close": b.low + b.deltaClose,
                    "volume": b.volume
                })
            df = pd.DataFrame(bars)
            if not df.empty:
                df[["open", "high", "low", "close"]] = df[["open", "high", "low", "close"]] / 100000.0
                df.set_index("time", inplace=True)
                self.ohlcv_cache[symbol_name] = df
                print(f"✅ Cached OHLCV for {symbol_name}")
                self.run_inference(symbol_name)
        elif msg_type == ProtoOAExecutionEvent().payloadType:
            res = Protobuf.extract(message)
            print(f"⚡ EXECUTION EVENT: {res.executionType}")
    def subscribe_to_symbols(self):
        req = ProtoOASymbolsListReq()
        req.ctidTraderAccountId = self.account_id
        self.client.send(req).addErrback(lambda _: None)
    def fetch_historical_data(self):
        for symbol, s_id in self.symbol_ids.items():
            req = ProtoOAGetTrendbarsReq()
            req.ctidTraderAccountId = self.account_id
            req.period = ProtoOATrendbarPeriod.H1
            req.fromTimestamp = int((datetime.utcnow().timestamp() - (90 * 24 * 3600)) * 1000)
            req.toTimestamp = int(datetime.utcnow().timestamp() * 1000)
            req.symbolId = s_id
            self.client.send(req).addErrback(lambda _: None)
    def subscribe_to_spots(self):
        for symbol, s_id in self.symbol_ids.items():
            req = ProtoOASubscribeSpotsReq()
            req.ctidTraderAccountId = self.account_id
            req.symbolId.append(s_id)
            self.client.send(req).addErrback(lambda _: None)
            print(f"📡 Subscribed to Live Spot Feed for {symbol}")
    def run_inference(self, symbol):
        df = self.ohlcv_cache.get(symbol)
        if df is None or len(df) < 500:
            return
        print(f"🧠 Running V3 Ensemble Inference for {symbol}...")
        try:
            cfg = PipelineConfig(
                ticker=symbol,
                start="2000-01-01",
                end="2099-01-01",
                bars_df=df,
                run_validation=False
            )
            result = self.pipeline.run(cfg)
            if len(result.signals) > 0:
                last_sig = result.signals[-1]
                last_bar_index = result.n_bars - 1
                print(f"🚨 SIGNAL DETECTED: {symbol} -> {'LONG' if last_sig.direction > 0 else 'SHORT'} at {last_sig.entry_price}")
                s_id = self.symbol_ids.get(symbol)
                existing_pos = self.open_positions.get(s_id)
                desired_side = ProtoOATradeSide.BUY if last_sig.direction > 0 else ProtoOATradeSide.SELL
                if existing_pos and existing_pos["tradeSide"] == desired_side:
                    print(f"🛡️ FIREWALL: Already holding a {symbol} position in the same direction. Skipping duplicate.")
                else:
                    self.execute_trade(symbol, last_sig)
            else:
                print(f"💤 No signals found for {symbol}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"❌ Inference failed for {symbol}: {e}")
            traceback.print_exc()
    def execute_trade(self, symbol, sig):
        print(f"💸 Sending Market Order for {symbol}...")
        s_id = self.symbol_ids.get(symbol)
        if not s_id: return
        req = ProtoOANewOrderReq()
        req.ctidTraderAccountId = self.account_id
        req.symbolId = s_id
        req.orderType = ProtoOAOrderType.MARKET
        req.tradeSide = ProtoOATradeSide.BUY if sig.direction > 0 else ProtoOATradeSide.SELL
        req.volume = 100000
        multiplier = 1000 if "JPY" in symbol else 100000
        if sig.stop_loss is not None:
            sl_distance = abs(sig.entry_price - sig.stop_loss)
            req.relativeStopLoss = int(round(sl_distance * multiplier))
        if sig.take_profit is not None:
            tp_distance = abs(sig.entry_price - sig.take_profit)
            req.relativeTakeProfit = int(round(tp_distance * multiplier))
        self.client.send(req).addErrback(lambda _: None)
        print("✅ Order sent to cTrader Matching Engine.")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    from dotenv import load_dotenv
    load_dotenv()
    print("=======================================")
    print(" LATENT DIFFUSION-HMM LIVE BRIDGE (V3) ")
    print("=======================================")
    client_id = os.getenv("CTRADER_CLIENT_ID", "DUMMY")
    client_secret = os.getenv("CTRADER_CLIENT_SECRET", "DUMMY")
    account_id = int(os.getenv("CTRADER_ACCOUNT_ID", "1234567"))
    token = os.getenv("CTRADER_ACCESS_TOKEN", "DUMMY_TOKEN")
    bridge = CTraderLiveBridge(client_id, client_secret, account_id, token, mode="demo")
    try:
        from twisted.internet import reactor
        bridge.start()
        reactor.run()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("Stopping bridge...")
```

## File: orchestrators/dynamic_tester.py
```python
import sys
import os
SCRIPT_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
ROOT_DIR = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(SCRIPT_DIR, ".."))
sys.path.insert(0, ROOT_DIR)
import json
import argparse
import config
import time
import subprocess
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime
try:
    import yfinance as yf
except ImportError:
    print("yfinance not found. Installing...")
    subprocess.run([sys.executable, "-m", "pip", "install", "yfinance"], check=True)
    import yfinance as yf
def get_local_data_path(ticker: str) -> str:
    file_path = os.path.join(ROOT_DIR, "data", f"{ticker.lower()}_1h.csv")
    if not os.path.exists(file_path):
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"Local data not found at {file_path}. Please run data_manager.py first.")
    return file_path
def run_backtest(csv_path: str, ticker: str):
    print(f"\n⚙️  Running Latent Diffusion Backtest Engine on {ticker}...")
    result_path = os.path.join(config.DYNAMIC_DIR, f"{ticker.lower()}_dynamic_results.json")
    env = os.environ.copy()
    env["HMM_STOP_LOSS_ATR"] = "4.0"
    env["HMM_TAKE_PROFIT_ATR"] = "8.0"
    env["STRATEGY_MODE"] = "MOMENTUM"
    env["TIMEFRAME"] = "1H"
    env["TIME_EXIT_BARS"] = "24"
    env["FOREX_RESULTS_PATH"] = os.path.abspath(result_path)
    t0 = time.time()
    engine_path = os.path.join(ROOT_DIR, "v3_engine", "engine", "reports.py")
    proc = subprocess.run(
        [sys.executable, engine_path, csv_path],
        env=env,
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    if proc.returncode != 0:
        print("❌ Backtest Engine Failed!")
        print(proc.stderr)
        return None
    print(f"✅ Backtest completed in {time.time() - t0:.1f}s")
    if not os.path.exists(result_path):
        print("❌ Results JSON not found.")
        return None
    with open(result_path, "r") as f:
        return json.load(f)
def print_tearsheet(data: dict, ticker: str):
    print("\n" + "="*50)
    print(f"  📊 TEAR SHEET: {ticker}")
    print("="*50)
    scenarios = data.get("pip_scenarios", {})
    gross_key = next((k for k in scenarios.keys() if "gross" in k), None)
    gross = scenarios.get(gross_key, {}) if gross_key else {}
    trades = gross.get("n_trades", 0)
    win_rate = gross.get("win_rate_pct", 0.0)
    pf = gross.get("profit_factor", 0.0)
    sr = gross.get("sharpe_ratio", 0.0)
    ret = gross.get("total_ret_pct", 0.0)
    print(f"Total Trades : {trades}")
    print(f"Win Rate     : {win_rate:.1f}%")
    print(f"Profit Factor: {pf:.2f}")
    print(f"Sharpe Ratio : {sr:+.2f}")
    print(f"Total Return : {ret:+.1f}%")
    if trades == 0:
        print("\n⚠️  WARNING: Strategy generated 0 valid setups. Div/0 aborted.")
    elif sr > 0.4:
        print("\n✅ VERDICT: EXCELLENT (ADMITTED)")
    else:
        print("\n❌ VERDICT: POOR EDGE (REJECTED)")
    print("="*50 + "\n")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Latent Diffusion Dynamic Tester")
    parser.add_argument("--ticker", required=True, help="Ticker symbol (e.g. SPY, EURUSD)")
    args = parser.parse_args()
    ticker = args.ticker.upper()
    import tempfile
    try:
        csv_path = get_local_data_path(ticker)
        print(f"✅ Found local pristine data for {ticker} at {csv_path}")
        results = run_backtest(csv_path, ticker)
        if results:
            print_tearsheet(results, ticker)
        os.remove(csv_path)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Pipeline Error: {str(e)}")
```

## File: orchestrators/ensemble_pipeline.py
```python
import sys
import os
SCRIPT_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
ROOT_DIR = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(SCRIPT_DIR, ".."))
sys.path.insert(0, ROOT_DIR)
import json, glob, time
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime
import warnings
import logging
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
logging.getLogger('matplotlib').setLevel(logging.ERROR)
logging.getLogger('matplotlib.font_manager').disabled = True
import config
DATA_DIR         = config.DATA_DIR
STRATEGY_MODE    = config.STRATEGY_MODE
TIMEFRAME        = config.WF_TIMEFRAME
STOP_LOSS_ATR    = config.ATR_SL_MULT
TAKE_PROFIT_ATR  = config.ATR_TP_MULT
TIME_EXIT_BARS   = config.TIME_EXIT_BARS
INITIAL_EQUITY   = config.INITIAL_EQUITY
RESULTS_DIR      = config.ENSEMBLE_DIR
SHARPE_FIREWALL  = config.ENSEMBLE_SHARPE_FIREWALL
HALF_KELLY_RISK  = config.ENSEMBLE_HALF_KELLY_RISK
USE_CACHED       = False
def _sep(title: str = "", width: int = 74) -> None:
    if title:
        pad = max(0, width - len(title) - 2)
        left = pad // 2
        right = pad - left
        print(f"{'─'*left} {title} {'─'*right}")
    else:
        print("─" * width)
def process_asset(csv_path, tmp_dir):
    import sys, os, time, numpy as np
    engine_path = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "v3_engine"))
    if engine_path not in sys.path:
        sys.path.insert(0, engine_path)
    import engine.reports as forex_tearsheet
    ticker = os.path.basename(csv_path).replace("_daily.csv", "").replace("_1h.csv", "").upper()
    result_path = os.path.join(tmp_dir, f"{ticker.lower()}_results.json")
    t0 = time.time()
    params = {
        "STOP_LOSS_ATR": STOP_LOSS_ATR,
        "TAKE_PROFIT_ATR": TAKE_PROFIT_ATR,
        "TIME_EXIT_BARS": TIME_EXIT_BARS,
        "HMM_WF_OOS_BARS": "240",
        "VETO_THRESHOLD": "0.70"
    }
    try:
        os.environ["FOREX_RESULTS_PATH"] = os.path.abspath(result_path)
        os.environ["TIMEFRAME"] = TIMEFRAME
        os.environ["HMM_WF_TRAIN_BARS"] = "1512"
        import io
        from contextlib import redirect_stdout
        with io.StringIO() as buf, redirect_stdout(buf):
            data = forex_tearsheet.run_tearsheet_dynamic(csv_path, params)
        elapsed = time.time() - t0
        scenarios = data.get("pip_scenarios", {})
        gross_key = next((k for k in scenarios.keys() if "gross" in k), None)
        gross = scenarios.get(gross_key, {}) if gross_key else {}
        n_trades   = gross.get("n_trades", 0)
        win_rate   = gross.get("win_rate_pct", 0)
        sharpe     = gross.get("sharpe_ratio", 0)
        pf         = gross.get("profit_factor", 0)
        total_ret  = gross.get("total_ret_pct", 0)
        returns    = np.array(gross.get("returns_array", []))
        result_dict = {
            "returns": returns, "n_trades": n_trades,
            "win_rate": win_rate, "sharpe": sharpe,
            "pf": pf, "total_ret": total_ret,
            "trades": data.get("trade_log", []),
        }
        summary_dict = {
            "ticker": ticker, "trades": n_trades,
            "win_rate": win_rate, "sharpe": sharpe,
            "pf": pf, "return": total_ret,
        }
        return ticker, True, elapsed, (result_dict, summary_dict), None
    except Exception as e:
        err_elapsed = time.time() - t0 if 't0' in locals() else 0.0
        return ticker, False, err_elapsed, None, str(e)
def main():
    import glob, time, os, argparse
    import pandas as pd
    from datetime import datetime
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    parser.add_argument("--split", choices=["train", "test", "all"], default="all", help="Data split to run (train = pre-OOS, test = post-OOS, all = full dataset)")
    args = parser.parse_args()
    wall_t0 = time.time()
    print("=" * 74)
    print(f"  LATENT DIFFUSION-HMM v3.0 — ENSEMBLE PORTFOLIO ENGINE ({args.split.upper()} SPLIT)")
    print(f"  Execution Time: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
    print()
    run_id = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
    tmp_dir = os.path.join(RESULTS_DIR, f".tmp_{run_id}")
    os.makedirs(tmp_dir, exist_ok=True)
    print(f"  Strategy: {STRATEGY_MODE}  |  TF: {TIMEFRAME}")
    print(f"  Risk: SL={STOP_LOSS_ATR}×ATR  TP={TAKE_PROFIT_ATR}×ATR  TimeExit={TIME_EXIT_BARS}b")
    print("=" * 74)
    print()
    csv_files = sorted(glob.glob(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "*_1h.csv")))
    if not csv_files:
        print("✗ No *_1h.csv files found in data/. Run download_basket.sh first.")
        return
    _sep(f"PHASE 1 — DISCOVERED {len(csv_files)} ASSETS")
    for f in csv_files:
        ticker = os.path.basename(f).replace("_daily.csv", "").upper()
        size_kb = os.path.getsize(f) / 1024
        print(f"  {ticker:>10}  →  {f}  ({size_kb:.0f} KB)")
    print()
    os.makedirs(RESULTS_DIR, exist_ok=True)
    asset_results = {}
    asset_summaries = []
    _sep(f"PHASE 2 — RUNNING {len(csv_files)} WALK-FORWARD BACKTESTS")
    print()
    import concurrent.futures
    futures = []
    with concurrent.futures.ProcessPoolExecutor(max_workers=os.cpu_count() or 8) as executor:
        for csv_path in csv_files:
            target_csv = csv_path
            if args.split != "all":
                df = pd.read_csv(csv_path)
                for col_name in ["timestamp", "datetime", "time", "date"]:
                    if col_name in df.columns:
                        if pd.api.types.is_numeric_dtype(df[col_name]):
                            dt_col = pd.to_datetime(df[col_name], unit="ms")
                        else:
                            dt_col = pd.to_datetime(df[col_name])
                        break
                if args.split == "train":
                    df = df[dt_col < pd.Timestamp(config.OOS_START_DATE)]
                elif args.split == "test":
                    df = df[dt_col >= pd.Timestamp("2022-01-01")]
                if df.empty:
                    print(f"  [!] {os.path.basename(csv_path)} is empty after {args.split} split. Skipping.")
                    continue
                target_csv = os.path.join(tmp_dir, f"{args.split}_" + os.path.basename(csv_path))
                df.to_csv(target_csv, index=False)
            futures.append(executor.submit(process_asset, target_csv, tmp_dir))
        completed = 0
        for future in concurrent.futures.as_completed(futures):
            completed += 1
            ticker, success, elapsed, payload, err = future.result()
            if success:
                res_d, sum_d = payload
                asset_results[ticker] = res_d
                asset_summaries.append(sum_d)
                status = "✓" if sum_d['sharpe'] > 0 else "─"
                print(f"  [{completed:>2}/{len(csv_files)}] {ticker:<8} {status}  trades={sum_d['trades']:>3}  WR={sum_d['win_rate']:>5.1f}%  PF={sum_d['pf']:>5.2f}  SR={sum_d['sharpe']:>+6.2f}  Ret={sum_d['return']:>+6.1f}%  ({elapsed:.1f}s)")
            else:
                print(f"  [{completed:>2}/{len(csv_files)}] {ticker:<8} ✗ FAILED ({elapsed:.1f}s) {err}")
    print()
    if not asset_results:
        print("✗ No assets produced valid results. Cannot build portfolio.")
        return
    _sep(f"PHASE 2.5 — SHARPE FIREWALL (min SR > {SHARPE_FIREWALL})")
    print()
    filtered_results = {}
    rejected = []
    for ticker, data in asset_results.items():
        if data.get("n_trades", 0) < 10:
            rejected.append(ticker)
            print(f"  ✗ {ticker:<10} TRADES={data.get('n_trades', 0):<3} → REJECTED (Insufficient trades)")
        elif data["sharpe"] >= SHARPE_FIREWALL:
            filtered_results[ticker] = data
            print(f"  ✓ {ticker:<10} SR={data['sharpe']:>+.2f}  PF={data['pf']:>.2f}  → ADMITTED")
        else:
            rejected.append(ticker)
            print(f"  ✗ {ticker:<10} SR={data['sharpe']:>+.2f}  PF={data['pf']:>.2f}  → REJECTED")
    print()
    print(f"  Admitted: {len(filtered_results)} / {len(asset_results)}")
    print(f"  Rejected: {len(rejected)} ({', '.join(rejected)})")
    print()
    if not filtered_results:
        print("✗ No assets passed the Sharpe Firewall. Loosen the threshold.")
        return
    asset_results = filtered_results
    _sep(f"PHASE 3 — CONCENTRATED PORTFOLIO ({len(asset_results)} assets)")
    max_len = max(len(v["returns"]) for v in asset_results.values())
    returns_df = pd.DataFrame()
    for ticker, data in asset_results.items():
        r = data["returns"]
        if len(r) < max_len:
            r = np.concatenate([r, np.zeros(max_len - len(r))])
        returns_df[ticker] = r
    N = len(asset_results)
    rolling_std = returns_df.rolling(window=20, min_periods=1).std().shift(1).fillna(1.0)
    rolling_std = rolling_std.replace(0, np.nan).bfill().fillna(1e-6)
    inv_vol = 1.0 / rolling_std
    weights = inv_vol.div(inv_vol.sum(axis=1), axis=0).fillna(1.0 / len(returns_df.columns))
    returns_df["PORTFOLIO"] = (returns_df * weights).sum(axis=1)
    port_returns = returns_df["PORTFOLIO"].values
    port_cum     = np.cumprod(1 + port_returns)
    total_trades = sum(v["n_trades"] for v in asset_results.values())
    total_wins   = sum(
        int(v["n_trades"] * v["win_rate"] / 100)
        for v in asset_results.values()
    )
    port_win_rate = (total_wins / total_trades * 100) if total_trades > 0 else 0
    ann_factor = config.ANN_FACTOR
    port_mean   = np.mean(port_returns) * ann_factor
    port_std    = np.std(port_returns, ddof=1) * np.sqrt(ann_factor)
    port_sharpe = port_mean / port_std if port_std > 0 else 0.0
    port_cum_max = np.maximum.accumulate(port_cum)
    port_dd      = (port_cum / port_cum_max - 1) * 100
    port_mdd     = np.min(port_dd)
    years = len(port_returns) / ann_factor
    port_total_ret = (port_cum[-1] - 1) * 100
    port_cagr      = ((port_cum[-1]) ** (1 / years) - 1) * 100 if years > 0 else 0
    final_equity = INITIAL_EQUITY * port_cum[-1]
    risk_per_trade = HALF_KELLY_RISK
    max_simultaneous = N
    risk_per_trade_scaled = risk_per_trade / max_simultaneous
    print(f"  Assets in portfolio : {N}")
    print(f"  Total portfolio trades: {total_trades}")
    print(f"  Aggregate Win Rate : {port_win_rate:.1f}%")
    print(f"  Half-Kelly Risk    : {risk_per_trade*100:.1f}% per trade → {risk_per_trade_scaled*100:.2f}% scaled (1/{N})")
    print()
    _sep("CONCENTRATED PORTFOLIO PERFORMANCE (Equal-Weight, Gross)")
    print(f"  {'Metric':<28} {'Value':>12}")
    print(f"  {'─'*28} {'─'*12}")
    print(f"  {'Total Return':<28} {port_total_ret:>+11.1f}%")
    print(f"  {'CAGR':<28} {port_cagr:>+11.1f}%")
    print(f"  {'Max Drawdown':<28} {port_mdd:>+11.1f}%")
    print(f"  {'Calmar Ratio':<28} {abs(port_cagr/port_mdd) if port_mdd != 0 else 0:>+11.2f}")
    print(f"  {'Sharpe Ratio':<28} {port_sharpe:>+11.2f}")
    print(f"  {'Final Equity':<28} ${final_equity:>10,.0f}")
    print()
    _sep("PER-ASSET LEADERBOARD")
    print(f"  {'Ticker':<10} {'Trades':>7} {'WinRate':>8} {'PF':>6} {'Sharpe':>8} {'Return':>8}")
    print(f"  {'─'*10} {'─'*7} {'─'*8} {'─'*6} {'─'*8} {'─'*8}")
    for s in sorted(asset_summaries, key=lambda x: x["sharpe"], reverse=True):
        if s["trades"] < 10 or s["pf"] > 1e6:
            continue
        marker = "★" if s["sharpe"] > 0.5 else "─"
        print(f"  {marker} {s['ticker']:<8} {s['trades']:>6} {s['win_rate']:>7.1f}% {s['pf']:>5.2f} {s['sharpe']:>+7.2f} {s['return']:>+7.1f}%")
    print()
    _sep("PHASE 5 — LAYER 6 PORTFOLIO VALIDATION")
    passes = 0
    total_tests = 5
    sr_pass = port_sharpe > 0.5
    passes += int(sr_pass)
    print(f"  6.1 Portfolio Sharpe Ratio           SR={port_sharpe:>+.2f}  {'PASS ✓' if sr_pass else 'FAIL ✗'}")
    from arch.bootstrap import StationaryBootstrap
    def sharpe_stat(returns):
        s = np.std(returns, ddof=1)
        return np.mean(returns) / s * np.sqrt(config.ANN_FACTOR) if s > 0 else 0.0
    bs = StationaryBootstrap(20, port_returns, seed=42)
    res = bs.apply(func=sharpe_stat, reps=10000)
    actual_sr = sharpe_stat(port_returns)
    mc_p = (res >= actual_sr).mean()
    mc_pass = mc_p < 0.05
    test_name = "Block Bootstrap Permutation"
    passes += int(mc_pass)
    print(f"  6.2 {test_name:<31} p={mc_p:.4f}  {'PASS ✓' if mc_pass else 'FAIL ✗'}")
    from scipy import stats
    T = len(port_returns)
    dsr_z = (port_sharpe * np.sqrt(T)) / np.sqrt(1 + 0.5 * port_sharpe**2)
    dsr_p = 1 - stats.norm.cdf(dsr_z)
    dsr_pass = dsr_p < 0.05
    passes += int(dsr_pass)
    print(f"  6.3 Deflated Sharpe Ratio            z={dsr_z:>+.2f}  p={dsr_p:.4f}  {'PASS ✓' if dsr_pass else 'FAIL ✗'}")
    n_pass = total_trades >= 30
    passes += int(n_pass)
    print(f"  6.4 Trade Count Sufficiency           N={total_trades}  {'PASS ✓' if n_pass else 'FAIL ✗'}")
    mdd_pass = abs(port_mdd) < 20
    passes += int(mdd_pass)
    print(f"  6.5 Max Drawdown Constraint          MDD={port_mdd:>+.1f}%  {'PASS ✓' if mdd_pass else 'FAIL ✗'}")
    print()
    print(f"  ══════════  {passes}/{total_tests} LAYER 6 TESTS PASSED  ══════════")
    print()
    if passes >= 4:
        verdict = "✓ VERDICT: INSTITUTIONAL GRADE — DEPLOY TO PAPER TRADING"
    elif passes >= 2:
        verdict = "~ VERDICT: MARGINAL — NEEDS FURTHER REFINEMENT"
    else:
        verdict = "✗ VERDICT: WASTE — SCRAP THE STRATEGY"
    _sep(verdict)
    print(f"  Portfolio Sharpe {port_sharpe:>+.2f}  |  Total Trades {total_trades}  |  MDD {port_mdd:.1f}%  |  WinRate {port_win_rate:.1f}%")
    _sep()
    ensemble_payload = {
        "run_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
        "n_assets": N,
        "total_trades": total_trades,
        "portfolio_sharpe": float(port_sharpe),
        "portfolio_total_return_pct": float(port_total_ret),
        "portfolio_cagr_pct": float(port_cagr),
        "portfolio_max_drawdown_pct": float(port_mdd),
        "portfolio_win_rate_pct": float(port_win_rate),
        "final_equity": float(final_equity),
        "layer6_passes": passes,
        "per_asset": asset_summaries,
    }
    ensemble_output = os.path.join(tmp_dir, "ensemble_results.json")
    with open(ensemble_output, "w") as f:
        json.dump(ensemble_payload, f, indent=2)
    try:
        import quantstats as qs
        dates = pd.date_range(end=datetime.now(), periods=len(port_returns), freq='B')
        qs_series = pd.Series(port_returns, index=dates)
        qs_path = os.path.join(config.TEARSHEETS_DIR, f"ensemble_tearsheet_{run_id}.html")
        qs.reports.html(qs_series, output=qs_path, title="Ensemble Portfolio Tear Sheet")
    except Exception as e:
        pass
    print(f"  Total wall-clock time: {time.time()-wall_t0:.1f}s")
    print()
    final_dir = os.path.join(RESULTS_DIR, f"run_{run_id}")
    os.rename(tmp_dir, final_dir)
    print(f"\n  ✅ Results permanently saved to: {final_dir}/")
    print(f"  Run ID: {run_id}")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

## File: orchestrators/grid_search.py
```python
import os, sys
_root = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '../../'))
if _root not in sys.path: sys.path.insert(0, _root)
import config
import sys
import os
SCRIPT_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
ROOT_DIR = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(SCRIPT_DIR, ".."))
sys.path.insert(0, ROOT_DIR)
import json, time
import itertools
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
import concurrent.futures
import subprocess
from datetime import datetime
import glob
import json
SCALE_INVARIANT_ASSETS = [
    "EURUSD", "GBPUSD", "USDJPY", "USDCHF", "AUDUSD", "NZDUSD", "USDCAD",
    "EURGBP", "AUDNZD", "AUDCAD", "EURCHF", "GBPCHF", "EURNOK", "EURSEK", "NOKSEK",
    "NZDCAD", "AUDCHF", "NZDCHF", "CADCHF", "EURAUD", "EURCAD", "GBPAUD",
    "CHFJPY", "CADJPY", "GBPCAD", "GBPNZD"
]
ensemble_runs = sorted(glob.glob("results/ensemble_results/run_*/ensemble_results.json"))
if ensemble_runs:
    try:
        with open(ensemble_runs[-1], 'r') as f:
            edata = json.load(f)
            winning = []
            for asset in edata.get("per_asset", []):
                if asset["sharpe"] >= 0.40:
                    ticker_clean = asset["ticker"].split("/")[-1].split("_")[0].upper()
                    winning.append(ticker_clean)
            if winning:
                SCALE_INVARIANT_ASSETS = winning
                print(f"Loaded {len(SCALE_INVARIANT_ASSETS)} Winning Assets from Baseline Ensemble!")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Warning: Failed to load ensemble winners: {e}")
DATA_DIR = config.DATA_DIR
RESULTS_DIR = config.GRID_DIR
TMP_BASE = os.path.join(RESULTS_DIR, ".tmp_grid")
os.environ.setdefault("HMM_N_ITER", "30")
os.environ.setdefault("HMM_VERBOSE", "0")
os.environ.setdefault("TIMEFRAME", "1H")
os.environ.setdefault("HMM_WF_TRAIN_BARS", "1512")
GRID = config.GRID_SEARCH_PARAMS
SLIPPAGE_PENALTY_KEY = config.GRID_SLIPPAGE_KEY
def get_combinations(grid):
    keys = list(grid.keys())
    values = list(grid.values())
    for prod in itertools.product(*values):
        yield dict(zip(keys, prod))
def _sep(title: str = "", width: int = 74) -> None:
    if title:
        pad = max(0, width - len(title) - 2)
        left = pad // 2
        right = pad - left
        print(f"{'─'*left} {title} {'─'*right}")
    else:
        print("─" * width)
def process_asset(csv_path, tmp_dir, params):
    import sys, os, numpy as np
    engine_path = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "v3_engine"))
    if engine_path not in sys.path:
        sys.path.insert(0, engine_path)
    import forex_tearsheet
    ticker = os.path.basename(csv_path).replace("_daily.csv", "").replace("_1h.csv", "").upper()
    try:
        os.environ["FOREX_RESULTS_PATH"] = os.path.join(tmp_dir, f"{ticker}_results.json")
        import io
        from contextlib import redirect_stdout
        with io.StringIO() as buf, redirect_stdout(buf):
            data = forex_tearsheet.run_tearsheet_dynamic(csv_path, params)
        scenarios = data.get("pip_scenarios", {})
        slip_key = next((k for k in scenarios.keys() if SLIPPAGE_PENALTY_KEY in k), None)
        if not slip_key:
            slip_key = next((k for k in scenarios.keys() if "0.1%" in k or "0.05%" in k), list(scenarios.keys())[-1])
        metrics = scenarios.get(slip_key, {})
        returns = np.array(metrics.get("returns_array", []))
        return ticker, True, {
            "returns": returns,
            "sharpe": metrics.get("sharpe_ratio", 0),
            "win_rate": metrics.get("win_rate_pct", 0),
            "trades": metrics.get("n_trades", 0)
        }
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  [Error in worker] {ticker}: {e}")
        return ticker, False, None
def calculate_psr_cpcv(agg_rets):
    import sys, os
    engine_path = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "v3_engine", "engine"))
    if engine_path not in sys.path:
        sys.path.insert(0, engine_path)
    from validation import cpcv
    if len(agg_rets) < 50: return 0.0
    def cpcv_simulate(train_idx, test_idx):
        return agg_rets[train_idx], agg_rets[test_idx]
    try:
        res = cpcv(cpcv_simulate, T=len(agg_rets), n_folds=config.CPCV_FOLDS)
        return float(res.psr)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  [CPCV Error] {e}")
        return 0.0
def main():
    os.makedirs(RESULTS_DIR, exist_ok=True)
    os.makedirs(TMP_BASE, exist_ok=True)
    combinations = list(get_combinations(GRID))
    total_trials = len(combinations)
    print("=" * 74)
    print("  LATENT DIFFUSION-HMM v3.0 — HYPERPARAMETER GRID SEARCH (STAGE 1)")
    print(f"  Total Combinations: {total_trials}")
    print(f"  Scale Invariant Assets: {SCALE_INVARIANT_ASSETS}")
    print("=" * 74)
    print()
    import glob
    csv_files = sorted(glob.glob(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "*_1h.csv")))
    if not csv_files:
        print("✗ No Stage 1 assets found in data/ directory.")
        return
    leaderboard = []
    with concurrent.futures.ProcessPoolExecutor(max_workers=os.cpu_count() or 8) as executor:
        for i, params in enumerate(combinations, 1):
            pct = (i / total_trials) * 100
            print(f"  [{i:>3}/{total_trials} | {pct:>5.1f}%] Testing Params: {params}")
            t0 = time.time()
            portfolio_returns = []
            total_trades = 0
            success_count = 0
            futures = [executor.submit(process_asset, csv, TMP_BASE, params) for csv in csv_files]
            for future in concurrent.futures.as_completed(futures):
                ticker, success, payload = future.result()
                if success and payload["trades"] > 0:
                    portfolio_returns.append(payload["returns"])
                    total_trades += payload["trades"]
                    success_count += 1
            elapsed = time.time() - t0
        if success_count > 0 and total_trades > 10:
            max_len = max(len(r) for r in portfolio_returns)
            agg_rets = np.zeros(max_len)
            for r in portfolio_returns:
                agg_rets[-len(r):] += r
            agg_rets = agg_rets / success_count
            daily_mean = agg_rets.mean()
            daily_vol = agg_rets.std() + 1e-9
            sr = daily_mean / daily_vol * np.sqrt(252)
            psr_val = calculate_psr_cpcv(agg_rets)
            leaderboard.append({
                "params": params,
                "sharpe": float(sr),
                "psr": float(psr_val),
                "trades": total_trades
            })
            status = "✓" if psr_val > 0.95 else "✗"
            print(f"         → {status} SR={sr:+.2f}  PSR={psr_val:.4f}  Trades={total_trades}  ({elapsed:.1f}s)")
        else:
            print(f"         → ─ No Trades Generated ({elapsed:.1f}s)")
    leaderboard.sort(key=lambda x: -x["psr"])
    print("\n" + "=" * 74)
    print("  🏆 STAGE 1 LEADERBOARD (TOP 10 DISTINCT ROBUST PARAMETERS)")
    print("=" * 74)
    top_10 = []
    seen_hash = set()
    for entry in leaderboard:
        if len(top_10) >= 10: break
        if entry["psr"] <= 0.95: continue
        shape_hash = f"{entry['params'].get('TIME_EXIT_BARS', '')}-{entry['params'].get('HMM_WF_OOS_BARS', '')}"
        if shape_hash in seen_hash and len(top_10) > 2:
            continue
        seen_hash.add(shape_hash)
        top_10.append(entry)
    for i, entry in enumerate(top_10, 1):
        print(f"  #{i} | PSR={entry['psr']:.4f} | SR={entry['sharpe']:+.2f} | Trades={entry['trades']}")
        print(f"      {entry['params']}\n")
    with open(os.path.join(RESULTS_DIR, "stage1_top10.json"), "w") as f:
        json.dump(top_10, f, indent=2)
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

## File: orchestrators/master_pipeline.py
```python
import sys
import os
import json
import time
import warnings
from datetime import datetime
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
from scipy import stats
warnings.filterwarnings("ignore")
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..")))
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "v3_engine")))
from engine.features import compute_feature_tensor
from engine.preprocess import Preprocessor
from engine.kalman import run_kalman_pipeline
from engine.hmm import TVTPHMM, STATE_LABELS
from engine.execution import TripleGate, KellyPositionSizer, compute_atr, SignalEngine
from engine.validation import walk_forward_cv, deflated_sharpe_ratio, transaction_cost_sensitivity, cpcv, _sharpe_ratio, _max_drawdown, COST_SCENARIOS
import config
import glob
TARGET_ASSETS = glob.glob("data/*_1h*.csv")
if not TARGET_ASSETS:
    print("WARNING: No data/*_1h.csv files found. Ensure you have downloaded data.")
STRATEGY_MODE = config.STRATEGY_MODE
EXECUTION_MODE = "WALK_FORWARD"
REGIME_CONFIDENCE = config.HMM_REGIME_CONF_THRESHOLD
MOMENTUM_Z_SCORE = 0.0
VOLUME_DELTA = 0.0
STOP_LOSS_ATR = config.ATR_SL_MULT_TREND
TAKE_PROFIT_ATR = config.ATR_TP_MULT_TREND
TIMEFRAME = config.TIMEFRAME
TIME_EXIT_BARS = config.TIME_EXIT_BARS
OOS_START = "2023-01-01"
def _sep(title: str = "", width: int = 74) -> None:
    if title:
        pad = max(0, width - len(title) - 2)
        left = pad // 2
        right = pad - left
        print(f"{'─'*left} {title} {'─'*right}")
    else:
        print("─" * width)
def _pf(passes: bool) -> str:
    return "PASS ✓" if passes else "FAIL ✗"
def _run_single_math_test(asset_path):
    raw = pd.read_csv(asset_path)
    if "time" in raw.columns:
        if pd.api.types.is_numeric_dtype(raw["time"]):
            raw["Date"] = pd.to_datetime(raw["time"], unit="ms")
        else:
            raw["Date"] = pd.to_datetime(raw["time"])
    elif "timestamp" in raw.columns:
        if pd.api.types.is_numeric_dtype(raw["timestamp"]):
            raw["Date"] = pd.to_datetime(raw["timestamp"], unit="ms")
        else:
            raw["Date"] = pd.to_datetime(raw["timestamp"])
    elif "datetime" in raw.columns:
        if pd.api.types.is_numeric_dtype(raw["datetime"]):
            raw["Date"] = pd.to_datetime(raw["datetime"], unit="ms")
        else:
            raw["Date"] = pd.to_datetime(raw["datetime"])
    else:
        raw["Date"] = pd.to_datetime(raw.index)
    raw = raw.set_index("Date")
    raw.columns = [c.capitalize() for c in raw.columns]
    bars_df = raw[["Open", "High", "Low", "Close"]].copy()
    bars_df.columns = ["open", "high", "low", "close"]
    bars_df["volume"] = raw["Volume"] if "Volume" in raw.columns else np.nan
    bars_df = bars_df.tail(2000)
    features = compute_feature_tensor(bars_df)
    bars_df = bars_df.loc[features.index]
    preprocessor = Preprocessor()
    X_white = preprocessor.fit_transform(features)
    print(f"  [DEBUG] Data Funnel (X_white) | Min: {np.nanmin(X_white):.2f} | Max: {np.nanmax(X_white):.2f} | Mean: {np.nanmean(X_white):.2f}")
    clean_idx = np.where(~np.any(np.isnan(X_white), axis=1))[0]
    X_clean = X_white[clean_idx[:2000]]
    covariates = np.zeros((len(X_clean), 2))
    hmm = TVTPHMM(n_states=3, n_gmm=2, n_iter=15)
    hmm.fit(X_clean, covariates)
    preds = hmm.predict_proba(X_clean, covariates)
    print("HMM Latest Probabilities:", preds[-1])
    if np.any(np.isnan(preds[-1])):
        print("[FAIL] HMM math collapsed to NaN")
    elif abs(preds[-1][0] - 0.333) < 0.01:
        print("[FAIL] HMM collapsed to 33.3%")
    else:
        print("[PASS] HMM successfully isolated dynamic states.")
def run_math_test():
    for asset in TARGET_ASSETS:
        print(f"\n--- Running HMM Math Isolation Test on {asset} ---")
        try:
            _run_single_math_test(asset)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error testing {asset}: {e}")
def run_walk_forward_tearsheet():
    for asset in TARGET_ASSETS:
        print(f"--- Running Expanding Walk-Forward CV on {asset} ---")
        os.environ["HMM_STOP_LOSS_ATR"] = str(STOP_LOSS_ATR)
        os.environ["HMM_TAKE_PROFIT_ATR"] = str(TAKE_PROFIT_ATR)
        os.environ["STRATEGY_MODE"] = STRATEGY_MODE
        os.environ["TIMEFRAME"] = TIMEFRAME
        os.environ["TIME_EXIT_BARS"] = str(TIME_EXIT_BARS)
        from engine.reports import run_tearsheet_dynamic
        params = {
            "STOP_LOSS_ATR": STOP_LOSS_ATR,
            "TAKE_PROFIT_ATR": TAKE_PROFIT_ATR,
            "HMM_WF_OOS_BARS": 252,
            "VETO_THRESHOLD": REGIME_CONFIDENCE,
            "TIME_EXIT_BARS": TIME_EXIT_BARS
        }
        run_tearsheet_dynamic(asset, params)
if __name__ == '__main__':
    print('Initializing Latent Diffusion-HMM v3.0...')
    if EXECUTION_MODE == 'MATH_TEST':
        run_math_test()
    elif EXECUTION_MODE == 'WALK_FORWARD':
        run_walk_forward_tearsheet()
    elif EXECUTION_MODE == 'BLIND_OOS':
        run_blind_oos_firewall()
    elif EXECUTION_MODE == 'IC_TEST':
        run_ic_tester()
    else:
        print('Invalid Execution Mode.')
```

## File: orchestrators/stage2_global_test.py
```python
import sys
import os
SCRIPT_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
ROOT_DIR = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(SCRIPT_DIR, ".."))
sys.path.insert(0, ROOT_DIR)
import json, glob, time
import numpy as np
import concurrent.futures
import subprocess
import config
DATA_DIR = config.DATA_DIR
RESULTS_DIR = config.GRID_DIR
TMP_BASE = os.path.join(RESULTS_DIR, ".tmp_stage2")
STAGE1_FILE = os.path.join(RESULTS_DIR, "stage1_top10.json")
SLIPPAGE_PENALTY_KEY = "1.5 pip"
def process_asset(csv_path, tmp_dir, params):
    import sys, os, numpy as np
    engine_path = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "v3_engine"))
    if engine_path not in sys.path:
        sys.path.insert(0, engine_path)
    import engine.reports as forex_tearsheet
    ticker = os.path.basename(csv_path).replace("_daily.csv", "").replace("_1h.csv", "").upper()
    try:
        os.environ["FOREX_RESULTS_PATH"] = os.path.join(tmp_dir, f"{ticker}_results.json")
        import io
        from contextlib import redirect_stdout
        with io.StringIO() as buf, redirect_stdout(buf):
            data = forex_tearsheet.run_tearsheet_dynamic(csv_path, params)
        scenarios = data.get("pip_scenarios", {})
        slip_key = next((k for k in scenarios.keys() if SLIPPAGE_PENALTY_KEY in k), None)
        if not slip_key:
            slip_key = next((k for k in scenarios.keys() if "0.1%" in k or "0.05%" in k), list(scenarios.keys())[-1])
        metrics = scenarios.get(slip_key, {})
        return ticker, True, {
            "returns": np.array(metrics.get("returns_array", [])),
            "sharpe": metrics.get("sharpe_ratio", 0),
            "win_rate": metrics.get("win_rate_pct", 0),
            "trades": metrics.get("n_trades", 0)
        }
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  [Error in worker] {ticker}: {e}")
        return ticker, False, None
def main():
    if not os.path.exists(STAGE1_FILE):
        print(f"✗ Stage 1 results not found at {STAGE1_FILE}. Run grid_search.py first.")
        return
    with open(STAGE1_FILE, "r") as f:
        top_10 = json.load(f)
    csv_files = sorted(glob.glob(os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "*_1h.csv")))
    if not csv_files:
        print("✗ No assets found in data/.")
        return
    os.makedirs(TMP_BASE, exist_ok=True)
    os.environ.setdefault("TIMEFRAME", "1H")
    os.environ.setdefault("HMM_WF_TRAIN_BARS", "1512")
    print("=" * 74)
    print("  LATENT DIFFUSION-HMM v3.0 — GLOBAL STRESS TEST (STAGE 2)")
    print(f"  Testing Top {len(top_10)} parameters across all {len(csv_files)} assets.")
    print("=" * 74)
    print()
    final_leaderboard = []
    with concurrent.futures.ProcessPoolExecutor(max_workers=os.cpu_count() or 8) as executor:
        for i, entry in enumerate(top_10, 1):
            params = entry["params"]
            pct = (i / len(top_10)) * 100
            print(f"  [{i:>2}/{len(top_10)} | {pct:>5.1f}%] Testing Params: {params}")
            t0 = time.time()
            portfolio_returns = []
            total_trades = 0
            success_count = 0
            futures = [executor.submit(process_asset, csv, TMP_BASE, params) for csv in csv_files]
            for future in concurrent.futures.as_completed(futures):
                ticker, success, payload = future.result()
                if success and payload["trades"] > 0:
                    portfolio_returns.append(payload["returns"])
                    total_trades += payload["trades"]
                    success_count += 1
            elapsed = time.time() - t0
            if success_count > 0 and total_trades > 0:
                max_len = max(len(r) for r in portfolio_returns)
                agg_rets = np.zeros(max_len)
                for r in portfolio_returns:
                    agg_rets[-len(r):] += r
                agg_rets = agg_rets / success_count
                daily_mean = agg_rets.mean()
                daily_vol = agg_rets.std() + 1e-9
                sr = daily_mean / daily_vol * np.sqrt(config.ANN_FACTOR) if 'config' in sys.modules else daily_mean / daily_vol * np.sqrt(252)
                final_leaderboard.append({
                    "params": params,
                    "global_sharpe": float(sr),
                    "global_trades": total_trades,
                    "stage1_dsr_p": entry["dsr_p"]
                })
                print(f"         → Global SR={sr:+.2f}  Global Trades={total_trades}  ({elapsed:.1f}s)")
            else:
                print(f"         → ─ No Trades Generated ({elapsed:.1f}s)")
    final_leaderboard.sort(key=lambda x: x["global_sharpe"], reverse=True)
    print("\n" + "=" * 74)
    print("  🌍 STAGE 2 GLOBAL LEADERBOARD (THE ULTIMATE SURVIVORS)")
    print("=" * 74)
    for i, entry in enumerate(final_leaderboard, 1):
        print(f"  #{i} | Global SR={entry['global_sharpe']:+.2f} | Trades={entry['global_trades']}")
        print(f"      {entry['params']}\n")
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

## File: risk_engine/risk.py
```python
import os, sys
_root = os.path.abspath(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '..'))
if _root not in sys.path: sys.path.insert(0, _root)
import config
class RiskEngine:
    def __init__(self, initial_equity: float):
        self.initial_equity = initial_equity
        self.peak_equity = initial_equity
        self.current_equity = initial_equity
        self.open_positions = {}
        self.daily_start_equity = initial_equity
        self.daily_reset_date = None
        self.trading_halted = False
        self.halt_reason = ""
        self._kelly_history = []
    def update_equity(self, new_equity: float, current_date):
        self.current_equity = new_equity
        self.peak_equity = max(self.peak_equity, new_equity)
        if self.daily_reset_date != current_date:
            self.daily_start_equity = new_equity
            self.daily_reset_date = current_date
        daily_dd = (new_equity - self.daily_start_equity) / self.daily_start_equity
        total_dd = (new_equity - self.peak_equity) / self.peak_equity
        if daily_dd < -config.DAILY_DRAWDOWN_LIMIT:
            self.trading_halted = True
            self.halt_reason = f"Daily drawdown limit {config.DAILY_DRAWDOWN_LIMIT*100:.1f}% hit"
        if total_dd < -config.MAX_DRAWDOWN_LIMIT:
            self.trading_halted = True
            self.halt_reason = f"Max drawdown limit {config.MAX_DRAWDOWN_LIMIT*100:.1f}% hit"
    def evaluate(
        self,
        symbol: str,
        direction: int,
        p_final: float,
        atr: float,
        current_price: float,
        wasserstein_scale: float,
        regime: str,
    ) -> dict:
        if self.trading_halted:
            return {"action": "VETO", "reason": self.halt_reason}
        if p_final < config.LIVE_P_FINAL_THRESHOLD:
            return {"action": "VETO", "reason": f"p_final {p_final:.3f} < threshold"}
        if len(self.open_positions) >= config.MAX_SIMULTANEOUS_POSITIONS:
            return {"action": "VETO", "reason": f"Max {config.MAX_SIMULTANEOUS_POSITIONS} positions open"}
        if symbol in self.open_positions:
            return {"action": "VETO", "reason": f"Position already open for {symbol}"}
        kelly_f = self._compute_kelly(p_final)
        kelly_f = min(kelly_f, config.MAX_POSITION_FRACTION)
        kelly_f = kelly_f * wasserstein_scale
        if regime == "TREND":
            sl_mult = config.ATR_SL_MULT_TREND
            tp_mult = config.ATR_TP_MULT_TREND
        elif regime == "MEAN_REV":
            sl_mult = config.ATR_SL_MULT_MEAN_REV
            tp_mult = config.ATR_TP_MULT_MEAN_REV
        else:
            sl_mult = config.ATR_SL_MULT_COMPRESSION
            tp_mult = config.ATR_TP_MULT_COMPRESSION
        sl_distance = atr * sl_mult
        tp_distance = atr * tp_mult
        risk_amount = kelly_f * self.current_equity
        units = risk_amount / max(sl_distance, 1e-10)
        if direction == 1:
            stop_loss   = current_price - sl_distance
            take_profit = current_price + tp_distance
        else:
            stop_loss   = current_price + sl_distance
            take_profit = current_price - tp_distance
        return {
            "action": "EXECUTE",
            "symbol": symbol,
            "direction": direction,
            "units": units,
            "stop_loss": stop_loss,
            "take_profit": take_profit,
            "position_fraction": kelly_f,
            "kelly_f": kelly_f,
            "sl_distance": sl_distance,
            "tp_distance": tp_distance,
        }
    def register_position(self, symbol: str, position: dict):
        self.open_positions[symbol] = position
    def close_position(self, symbol: str, exit_price: float, exit_time):
        pos = self.open_positions.pop(symbol, None)
        if pos is None:
            return
        pnl = (exit_price - pos["entry_price"]) * pos["direction"] * pos["units"]
        self._kelly_history.append(pnl)
        if len(self._kelly_history) > config.KELLY_ESTIMATION_WINDOW:
            self._kelly_history.pop(0)
        self.update_equity(self.current_equity + pnl, exit_time.date())
    def _compute_kelly(self, p_final: float) -> float:
        if len(self._kelly_history) >= 30:
            wins = sum(1 for r in self._kelly_history if r > 0)
            win_rate = wins / len(self._kelly_history)
            avg_win = sum(r for r in self._kelly_history if r > 0) / max(wins, 1)
            avg_loss = abs(sum(r for r in self._kelly_history if r <= 0)) / max(len(self._kelly_history) - wins, 1)
            b = avg_win / max(avg_loss, 1e-10)
            full_kelly = (win_rate * b - (1 - win_rate)) / max(b, 1e-10)
            return max(0.0, full_kelly * config.HALF_KELLY_FRACTION)
        return max(0.0, (p_final - (1 - p_final)) * config.HALF_KELLY_FRACTION)
```
